BSTOD, ,BSOD NAMS PHUL PHYIN STOBS KYIS RAB BSKYOD PAS, ,SRID
ZHI'I DPAL 'BYOR LONGS SPYOD GANG

MCHOG DANG, ,GSANG SNGAGS LUNG RIGS MAN NGAG BSTAN BCOS SOGS, ,MA
LUS NYID KYI DRUNG DU 'DU BA'I PHYIR, ,MNGA' BDAG BTZAN PO SDE
YIS RAB BSGRUBS PA'I, ,MGYOGS 'GRO DPAL MO'I BU YI BLAD DOR GYI,
,GTAN TSIGS CHEN PO BSTAN

BCOS RAB GSAL BA, ,SHIN TU GSANG ZHES YANG YANG GDAMS PA 'DI,
,GSANG SNGAGS ZAB MOR SPYAD NA DNGOS GRUB THOB, ,'CHOL BAR SPYOD
PA MKHAS PA'I TSUL MIN PAS, ,TZANDAN TSUL DBANG KLU DBANG NOR BU
LTAR, ,NYAMS SU DON BZHES

DKOR MDZOD DU GZHAG GSOL, ,CES PA DANG BCAS PA 'DI DAG PHAG LO
ZLA BA DANG PO'I TSES GCIG GI NYIN, ,THOS PA CUNG ZAD 'DZIN PA MA
TI BHA DRAS GSOL PA PHYOGS KUN DU BDE LEGS KYIS GANG BAR GYUR
CIG, ,,
